###########################
# Russian Civil War Events
###########################

add_namespace = rcw_usfev

# Восстание забайкальских казаков (мятеж Семёнова)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1
	title = rcw_usfev.1.t
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.1.desc
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_all_russian_constituent_assembly_second_session_serfdom }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.1.desc_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_all_russian_constituent_assembly_second_session_serfdom }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.1.desc_2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_all_russian_constituent_assembly_second_session_serfdom
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_rus_kazaks_war
	
	trigger = {
		has_start_date < 1917.11.7
		tag = RUS
		BKL = { exists = no }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = BKL_revolt }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_cossacks_were_disbanded }
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77299 } set_nationality = BKL }
			BKL = {
				#transfer_state = 761
				#transfer_state = 1209
				transfer_state = 950
				#transfer_state = 951
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = PREV
								is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
								former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
								has_war_with = PREV
								is_in_faction_with = PREV
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_provisional_government_not_so_provisional }
				BKL = { load_focus_tree = Transbaikal_white_cossaks_late_focus transfer_state = 563 }
				else = {
					BKL = {
						remove_ideas = peasant_and_land_and_bread_question_0_5
						add_ideas = marching_army_idea
						set_cosmetic_tag = BKL_SMS
					}
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Kazach'ya brigada"
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1.a
		set_country_flag = BKL_revolt
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_provisional_government_not_so_provisional }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BKL
				type = annex_everything
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				BKL = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 100
						producer = JAP
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = artillery_equipment
						amount = 24
						producer = JAP
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Pekhotniy batalyon"
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
						support = {
							artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 100
						producer = FNG
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Miliceyskiy batalyon"
						regiments = {
							militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					add_manpower = 2000
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 200
						producer = BKL
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					capital_scope = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Yaponskiy pekhotniy otryad\" division_template = \"Pekhotniy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Kitayskaya miliciya\" division_template = \"Miliceyskiy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Kitayskaya miliciya\" division_template = \"Miliceyskiy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Mongolskaya brigada\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.01 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Otryad hunhuzov\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = ROOT
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = BKL
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = artillery_equipment
						amount = 5
						producer = BKL
					}
					add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_russian_volunteers_idea days = 182 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_right_oficers days = 365 }
					add_ideas = BKL_special_manchu_squad_idea
					add_country_leader_trait = ataman
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_capital = 950
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
					RUS = {
						declare_war_on = {
							target = BKL
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
				has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = BKL_revolt
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_provisional_government_not_so_provisional }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BKL
				type = annex_everything
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				BKL = {
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 100
						producer = JAP
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = artillery_equipment
						amount = 24
						producer = JAP
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Pekhotniy batalyon"
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
						support = {
							artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 100
						producer = FNG
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Miliceyskiy batalyon"
						regiments = {
							militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						}
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					add_manpower = 2000
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 200
						producer = BKL
					}
					division_template = {
						name = "Kavaleriyskaya brigada"
						regiments = {
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						}
					}
					capital_scope = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Yaponskiy pekhotniy otryad\" division_template = \"Pekhotniy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.5 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Kitayskaya miliciya\" division_template = \"Miliceyskiy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Kitayskaya miliciya\" division_template = \"Miliceyskiy batalyon\" start_experience_factor = 0.2 start_equipment_factor = 0.01 "
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Mongolskaya brigada\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.01 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = ROOT
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Otryad hunhuzov\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya brigada\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = ROOT
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = 500
						producer = BKL
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = artillery_equipment
						amount = 5
						producer = BKL
					}
					add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_russian_volunteers_idea days = 182 }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_right_oficers days = 365 }
					add_ideas = BKL_special_manchu_squad_idea
					add_country_leader_trait = ataman
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_capital = 950
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { OR = { has_completed_focus = RUS_struggle_against_counterrevolution NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus } } } }
					RUS = {
						declare_war_on = {
							target = BKL
							type = annex_everything
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		BKL = { change_tag_from = RUS }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1.c
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
				has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = BKL_revolt
		if = {

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.2
	title = rcw_usfev.2.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.2.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_czech_uprising
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = BKL
		controls_state = 566
		NOT = { owns_state = 566 }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.2.a
		transfer_state = 566
		add_state_core = 566
	}
}

###Восстание в Приморье (если Семёнов взял Владивосток)###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.12
	title = rcw_usfev.95.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.12.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_sibir_uprising
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_uprising } }
		tag = RUS
		BKL = { controls_state = 408 }
		PRM = { exists = no }
		SIB = { exists = no }
		CCA = { exists = no }
		RSS = { exists = no }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.95.a
		add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_threat_of_intervention value = 1 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 560
					state = 409
					state = 408
					state = 655
					state = 1034
					state = 1035
					state = 1036
					state = 1037
					state = 1038
					state = 1185
					state = 1186
				}
			}
			add_core_of = PRM
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = RUS
					is_owned_by = FER
					is_owned_by = HRB
				}
				OR = {
					state = 717
					state = 560
					state = 409
					state = 408
					state = 655
					state = 951
					state = 1034
					state = 1035
					state = 1036
					state = 1037
					state = 1038
					state = 1185
					state = 1186
				}
			}
			PRM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BKL
				is_core_of = PRM
			}
			remove_core_of = BKL
		}
		PRM = {
			PRM = { inherit_technology = RUS }
			add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
			remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
			load_oob = PRM_contra
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_uprising } }
				load_oob = PRM_czechoslovak_legion
			}
			RUS = { set_province_controller = 12559 load_oob = RUS_PRM_red_guard }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = national_syndicalism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = national_syndicalism popularity = 0.1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = PREV
							is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
							former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
							has_war_with = PREV
							is_in_faction_with = PREV
						}
					}
					set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
				}
			}
		}
		BKL = { PRM = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_dominion = yes } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = PRM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.95.b
		add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_threat_of_intervention value = 1 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 560
					state = 409
					state = 408
					state = 655
					state = 1034
					state = 1035
					state = 1036
					state = 1037
					state = 1038
					state = 1185
					state = 1186
				}
			}
			add_core_of = PRM
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = RUS
					is_owned_by = FER
					is_owned_by = HRB
				}
				OR = {
					state = 717
					state = 560
					state = 409
					state = 408
					state = 655
					state = 951
					state = 1034
					state = 1035
					state = 1036
					state = 1037
					state = 1038
					state = 1185
					state = 1186
				}
			}
			PRM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BKL
				is_core_of = PRM
			}
			remove_core_of = BKL
		}
		PRM = {
			PRM = { inherit_technology = RUS }
			add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
			remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes
			load_oob = PRM_contra
			if = {
				limit = { RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_uprising } }
				load_oob = PRM_czechoslovak_legion
			}
			RUS = { set_province_controller = 12559 load_oob = RUS_PRM_red_guard }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = national_syndicalism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = national_syndicalism popularity = 0.1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = PREV
							is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
							former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
							has_war_with = PREV
							is_in_faction_with = PREV
						}
					}
					set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
				}
			}
		}
		BKL = { PRM = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_dominion = yes } }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = PRM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		PRM = { change_tag_from = RUS }
	}
}

###Боевые дружины левых эсеров поднимают восстание, если они в составе КОМУЧ###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.13
	title = rcw_usfev.13.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.13.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_czech_uprising
	
	trigger = {
		tag = CCA
		has_war_with = RUS
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		has_country_flag = main_left_essers_is_here
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.13.a
		load_oob = CCA_left_esser_rise
		add_state_core = 398
		set_state_owner = 398
		add_state_core = 249
		set_state_owner = 249
		add_state_core = 239
		set_state_owner = 239
		add_state_core = 250
		set_state_owner = 250
		add_state_core = 252
		set_state_owner = 252
		add_state_core = 248
		set_state_owner = 248
		RUS = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19189 } set_nationality = CCA } }
	}
	
}

	}

# Восстание чехословацкого корпуса
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.15
	title = rcw_usfev.15.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.15.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_czech_uprising
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		has_country_flag = RUS_has_czechoslovak_legion
		NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_red_czechoslovak_legion }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_uprising }
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
		CCA = { exists = no }
		SIB = { exists = no }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = RUS_has_czechoslovak_legion
			clr_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_evac_progress
			set_equipment_fraction = 0.8
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77400 } set_nationality = SIB }
			add_to_variable = { var = global.RUS_threat_of_intervention value = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_3
					add_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_4
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_2
					add_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_1
					add_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_2
				}
			}
			release = TAN
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.15.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_uprising
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = BKL owns_state = 563 divisions_in_state = { size > 0 state = 563 } }
			BKL = { transfer_state = 563 }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 40
					state = 569
					state = 570
					state = 578
					state = 654
					state = 654
					state = 909
					
					state = 566
					state = 575
					state = 564
					state = 565
					state = 644
					state = 574
					
					state = 516
					state = 1043
					state = 567
					state = 568
					state = 571
					state = 1067
					state = 576
					state = 577
					state = 572
					state = 1103
					state = 573
					state = 582
					state = 652
					state = 651
					state = 1025
					
					state = 583
					state = 588
					state = 590
				}
			}
			add_core_of = SIB
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					any_country = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						PREV = { is_owned_by = PREV }
					}
				}
				OR = {
					state = 40

					state = 578

			remove_all_foreing_locked_templates_from_liberated_country = yes

				set_major = yes
				inherit_technology = ROOT
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.54 days = 60 }
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.56 days = 120 }
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SIB_right_oficers
					days = 200
				}
				set_country_flag = SIB_start_political_instability
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							tag = PREV
							is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
							former_russian_empire_baltic_states_country = yes
							has_war_with = PREV
							is_in_faction_with = PREV
						}
					}
					set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.15.b
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_uprising

						is_subject_of = ROOT
						PREV = { is_owned_by = PREV }
					}

				OR = {

# Свержение советской власти в Поволжье
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.16
	title = rcw_usfev.16.t
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.16.desc

		trigger = {
			NOT = { OCH = { OR = { controls_state = 251 controls_state = 651 } } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_all_russian_constituent_assembly_ended }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.16.desc_1
		trigger = {
			OCH = { OR = { controls_state = 251 controls_state = 651 } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.16.desc_2
		trigger = {
			NOT = { OCH = { OR = { controls_state = 251 controls_state = 651 } } }
			has_global_flag = RUS_all_russian_constituent_assembly_ended
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_sibir_uprising
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_czechoslovak_legion_uprising
			OCH = { OR = { controls_state = 251 controls_state = 651 } }
		}
		OR = {
			SIB = { exists = yes NOT = { has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism } }
			OCH = { OR = { controls_state = 251 controls_state = 651 } }
		}
		OR = {
			OCH = { OR = { controls_state = 251 controls_state = 651 } }
			has_global_flag = RUS_all_russian_constituent_assembly_ended
			has_country_flag = RUS_karaul_ustal
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 35

			factor = 0.01

		}
	}

		hidden_effect = {

				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_2
					add_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_3
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_1
					add_idea = RUS_collapse_of_railway_system_2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#КОМУЧ эсеров

					}

		text = rcw_usfev.18.desc

		trigger = {
			NOT = { SOV = { exists = yes OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism has_government = social_democracy } } }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.18.desc_1
		trigger = {
			SOV = { exists = yes OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism has_government = social_democracy } }
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_cca_esser
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.18.a
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = { exists = yes has_country_leader = { name = "Vladimir Lenin" ruling_only = yes } }
				random_list = {
					30 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 0
							has_country_flag = RUS_red_terror
						}
						modifier = {
							factor = 0.5
							has_completed_focus = RUS_vchk
						}
						country_event = { id = rcw_bolsheviks.131 days = 1 }
					}
					50 = {
						country_event = { id = rcw_bolsheviks.132 days = 1 }
					}
					20 = {
						modifier = {
							factor = 1.75
							has_completed_focus = RUS_vchk
						}
						country_event = { id = rcw_bolsheviks.133 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			
			random_country = {
				limit = { exists = yes NOT = { has_country_flag = Moisey_Uritskiy_dead } has_completed_focus = RUS_vchk }
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						country_event = { id = rcw_bolsheviks.134 days = 1 }
					}
					50 = {  }
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.26
	title = rcw_usfev.26.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.26.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sov_redarm
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.26.a
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = radical_socialism
					size = 0.4
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
				}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = CCA
					has_government = radical_socialism
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = CCA_CW
				set_stability = 0.9
				set_war_support = 0.8
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = CCA
						NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:CCA_CW }
					}
					declare_war_on = { target = event_target:CCA_CW type = annex_everything }
				}
				event_target:CCA_CW = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = {
								array = unrecognized_states
								value = ROOT.id
							}
						}
						set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { clear_global_event_target = CCA_CW }
			}
	}
}

# Сибирский ультиматум о передаче Челябинска, контроля над Уральским правительством, аннексии (КОМУЧ)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.44
	title = rcw_usfev.44.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.44.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rus_entente

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.44.a
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { SIB_pressure_CCA = 1 } }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SIB modifier = SIB_accept_CCA }
			SIB = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CCA modifier = SIB_accept }
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.46 days = 1 }
			}
			if = {
			limit = { URL = { exists = yes is_subject_of = SIB } }
			URL = {
				transfer_state = 572
				}
				else = {
					SIB = {
						transfer_state = 572
						add_state_core = 572
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { SIB_pressure_CCA = 2 } }
			SIB = {
				URL = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_integrated_puppet = yes }
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.46 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { SIB_pressure_CCA = 3 } }
			CCA = {
				every_unit_leader = {
						set_nationality = SIB
					}
			}
			SIB = {
				annex_country = {
					target = CCA
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = CCA }
					add_core_of = SIB
				}
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.46 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.44.b
		SIB = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.45 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.50
	title = rcw_usfev.50.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.50.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_moscow_peace
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.50.a
		set_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_reds_n_Siberia_peace
		every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = RUS
					OR = {
						tag = SIB
						is_in_faction_with = SIB
					}
				}
				white_peace = RUS
		}
		if = {
				limit = { OCH = { exists = yes } OR = { SIB = { controls_state = 651 } SIB = { controls_state = 251 } } }
				every_state = {
					limit = { OR = { is_core_of = OCH is_controlled_by = OCH } is_owned_by = RUS }
					OCH = { transfer_state = PREV }
					remove_core_of = RUS
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = RUS
						OR = {
							tag = OCH
							is_in_faction_with = OCH
						}
					}
					white_peace = RUS
				}

							state = 574

							state = 653

							state = 1209
							state = 573
							state = 582
							state = 651
							state = 652
							state = 717
							state = 40
							state = 569
							state = 570
							state = 578
							state = 654
							state = 909
							state = 581
							state = 911
						}
					}
					SIB = { transfer_state = PREV add_state_core = PREV }

		else_if = {
			limit = { SIB = { controls_state = 651 } }
			SIB = {

				}
				add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
				remove_ideas_with_trait = trade_laws
				add_ideas = free_trade
				add_ideas = SIB_hard_peace_idea
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = RUS
						OR = {
							state = 580
							state = 579
							state = 403
							state = 644
							state = 566
							state = 575
							state = 564
							state = 565
							state = 1041
							state = 563
							state = 572
							state = 1103
						}
					}
					SIB = { transfer_state = PREV add_state_core = PREV }
				}
				give_military_access = RUS
				remove_state_core = 398
				remove_state_core = 651
				remove_state_core = 652
				remove_state_core = 582
				remove_state_core = 573
				remove_state_core = 581
			}
			if = {
				limit = { PRM = { is_subject_of = SIB } }
				RUS = {
					annex_country = { 
						target = PRM 
						transfer_troops = no 
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { OCH = { is_subject_of = SIB } }
				RUS = {
					annex_country = { 
						target = OCH 
						transfer_troops = no 
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BKL = { is_subject_of = SIB } }
				RUS = {
					annex_country = { 
						target = BKL 
						transfer_troops = no 
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CCA = { is_subject_of = SIB } }
				RUS = {
					annex_country = { 
						target = CCA 
						transfer_troops = no 
					}
				}
			}
		}
		}
		every_state = { limit = { is_core_of = SIB is_owned_by = SIB } remove_core_of = RUS }
		every_state = { limit = { is_owned_by = SIB is_core_of = RUS  } RUS = { transfer_state = PREV.PREV } }
		every_state = { limit = { is_core_of = RUS } remove_core_of = SIB }
		every_state = { limit = { is_core_of = RUS } remove_claim_by = SIB }
		
			if = {
				limit = { KAZ = { exists = yes OR = { is_subject_of = SIB is_in_faction_with = SIB } } }
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = KAZ
						OR = {
							tag = RUS
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
						}
					}
					white_peace = KAZ
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = KAZ }
					KAZ = { transfer_state = PREV }
					remove_core_of = RUS
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { PRM = { exists = yes OR = { is_subject_of = SIB is_in_faction_with = SIB } } OR = { SIB = { controls_state = 651 } SIB = { controls_state = 251 } } }
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = PRM }
					PRM = { transfer_state = PREV }
					remove_core_of = RUS
				}
			}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.50.b
		if = {
			limit = { SIB = { controls_state = 251 } }
			add_war_support = -0.15
			add_political_power = -100
					else_if = {
						limit = { SIB = { controls_state = 651 } }
						add_war_support = -0.05
						add_political_power = -50
						}
			}
	}
}

			change_tag_from = SIB
			else = {

			}
		}
	}

		name = rcw_usfev.60.b
		trigger = {SIB = {exists = yes} NOT = {SIB = {has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism}}}
		every_country = {
			limit = {

					AND = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = TAN
					}
				}

		tag = SIB
		always = no
		surrender_progress > 0.4
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Alexandr Kolchak" }
			has_country_leader = { name = "Roman Fyodorovich von Ungern-Sternberg" }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.72.a
		#news_event
		random_list = {
		50 = {
		set_politics = {ruling_party = despotism elections_allowed = no}
		set_party_name = { ideology = despotism long_name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party }
		create_country_leader = { name = "Alexandr Kolchak" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Alexandr_Kolchak_supreme_ruler_ALT3.dds" expire = "1936.2.7" ideology = despotism_ideology traits = { moy_admiral warmonger goal_in_politics goal } }
		}
		50 = {
		add_political_power = -50
		}
		}
	}
	
}

# Восстание Политцентра (только Сибирь)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.73
	title = rcw_usfev.73.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.73.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sovarmy
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = SIB
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_Politcenter_fired }
		surrender_progress > 0.7
		NOT = { has_government = social_liberalism }
		NOT = { has_government = social_democracy }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = RCW_Politcenter_fired
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.73.a
		#news_event
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
				create_country_leader = { name = "Florian Fyodorovich" desc = "RUS_Florian_Fyodorovich_DESC" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Florian_Fyodorovich.dds" ideology = social_democracy_ideology traits = { } }
				else = {
					create_country_leader = { name = "Florian Fyodorovich" desc = "RUS_Florian_Fyodorovich_DESC" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Florian_Fyodorovich.dds" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = { } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { controls_state = 566 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = social_democracy
					size = 0.1
					capital = 566
					states = {
						566
					}
				}
				else = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = social_liberalism
						size = 0.1
						capital = 566
						states = {
							566
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 571 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = social_democracy
						size = 0.1
						capital = 571
						states = {
							571
						}
					}
					else = {
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = social_liberalism
							size = 0.1
							capital = 571
							states = {
								571
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = social_democracy
							size = 0.1
						}
						else = {
							start_civil_war = {
								ideology = social_liberalism
								size = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						OR = {
							has_government = social_democracy
							has_government = social_liberalism
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = Politcenter
					save_global_event_target_as = Politcenter
					set_stability = 0.9
					set_war_support = 0.8
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
							NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:Politcenter }
						}
						declare_war_on = { target = event_target:Politcenter type = annex_everything }
					}
			}
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { OR = { has_id = 92354 has_id = 92355 has_id = 88153 } }
				set_nationality = event_target:Politcenter
			}
			event_target:Politcenter = {
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = ROOT
					size = 1
					stockpile_ratio = 1
					army_ratio = 1
					navy_ratio = 1
					air_ratio = 1
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { OR = { has_id = 92354 has_id = 92355 has_id = 88153 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { any_country = { OR = { exists = yes exists = no } any_unit_leader = { has_id = 92356 } } }
					}
					create_corps_commander = { name = "Evgeniy Kolosov" id = 92356 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Evgeniy_Kolosov.dds" traits = { politically_connected } skill = 1 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 1 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { any_country = { OR = { exists = yes exists = no } any_unit_leader = { has_id = 92357 } } }
					}
					create_corps_commander = { name = "Nikolay Kalashnikov" id = 92357 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Nikolay_Kalashnikov.dds" traits = { politically_connected } skill = 1 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 1 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = unrecognized_states
							value = ROOT.id
						}
					}
					set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment_great_war
					amount = 3000
					producer = RUS
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = RUS
				}

						target = RGR
						type = annex_everything
					}

						target = BKL
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}

					declare_war_on = {
						target = RUS
						type = annex_everything
					}

# Разоружение чехословацкого легиона (Сибирь)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.74
	title = rcw_usfev.74.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.74.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_czechoslovakians
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.74.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_stability < 0.4
						check_variable = { party_popularity@ruling_party < 0.15 }
					}
					NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_Politcenter_fired }
				}
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.75 days = 1 }
				else = {
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
					}
					delete_unit_template_and_units = {
						division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment_great_war
						amount = 15000
						producer = RUS
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = support_equipment
						amount = 15000
						producer = RUS
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var = global.RCW_green_var_Siberia
						value = -1
					}
				}
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.1 }
			add_war_support = 0.1
			add_stability = 0.2
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = 0.2
			add_war_support = 0.1
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.1 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.1 }
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment_great_war
				amount = 15000
				producer = RUS
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = support_equipment
				amount = 15000
				producer = RUS
			}
		}
	}
}
# Второй чехословацкий мятеж (Сибирь; Политцентр)
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.75
	title = rcw_usfev.75.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.75.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_czech_uprising
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = RCW_Politcenter_fired
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.75.a
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.RCW_green_var_Siberia
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
				create_country_leader = { name = "Florian Fyodorovich" desc = "RUS_Florian_Fyodorovich_DESC" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Florian_Fyodorovich.dds" ideology = social_democracy_ideology traits = { } }
				else = {
					create_country_leader = { name = "Florian Fyodorovich" desc = "RUS_Florian_Fyodorovich_DESC" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Florian_Fyodorovich.dds" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = { } }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { controls_state = 566 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = social_democracy
					size = 0.1
					capital = 566
					states = {
						566
					}
				}
				else = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = social_liberalism
						size = 0.1
						capital = 566
						states = {
							566
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 571 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = social_democracy
						size = 0.1
						capital = 571
						states = {
							571
						}
					}
					else = {
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = social_liberalism
							size = 0.1
							capital = 571
							states = {
								571
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB }
						start_civil_war = {
							ideology = social_democracy
							size = 0.1
						}
						else = {
							start_civil_war = {
								ideology = social_liberalism
								size = 0.1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						OR = {
							has_government = social_democracy
							has_government = social_liberalism
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = Politcenter
					save_global_event_target_as = Politcenter
					set_stability = 0.9
					set_war_support = 0.8
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = ROOT
							NOT = { has_war_with = event_target:Politcenter }
						}
						declare_war_on = { target = event_target:Politcenter type = annex_everything }
					}
			}
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { OR = { has_id = 92354 has_id = 92355 has_id = 88153 } }
				set_nationality = event_target:Politcenter
			}
			event_target:Politcenter = {
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = ROOT
					size = 1
					stockpile_ratio = 1
					army_ratio = 1
					navy_ratio = 1
					air_ratio = 1
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { OR = { has_id = 92354 has_id = 92355 has_id = 88153 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { any_country = { OR = { exists = yes exists = no } any_unit_leader = { has_id = 92356 } } }
					}
					create_corps_commander = { name = "Evgeniy Kolosov" id = 92356 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Evgeniy_Kolosov.dds" traits = { politically_connected } skill = 1 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 1 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { any_country = { OR = { exists = yes exists = no } any_unit_leader = { has_id = 92357 } } }
					}
					create_corps_commander = { name = "Nikolay Kalashnikov" id = 92357 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Nikolay_Kalashnikov.dds" traits = { politically_connected } skill = 1 attack_skill = 1 defense_skill = 1 planning_skill = 1 logistics_skill = 1 }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_array = {
							array = unrecognized_states
							value = ROOT.id
						}
					}
					set_THIS_country_non_recognize_PREV = yes
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment_great_war
					amount = 3000
					producer = RUS
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = 500
					producer = RUS
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = RGR } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RGR
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = BKL } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = BKL
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = RUS } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RUS
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Partiynaya druzjina"
					regiments = {
						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					}
					support = {
					}
					is_locked = no
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Partiynaya druzjina\" division_template = \"Partiynaya druzjina\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = CONTROLLER
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Partiynaya druzjina\" division_template = \"Partiynaya druzjina\" start_experience_factor = 0.3 start_equipment_factor = 1"
						owner = CONTROLLER
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona" }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona" }
				event_target:Politcenter = {
					division_template = {
						name = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"		# Elite
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
						support = {
							recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							field_hospital = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						}
						priority = 2
						is_locked = yes
					}
					random_owned_state = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"2-ya Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
							owner = CONTROLLER
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Brigada Radola Gajdi Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
							owner = CONTROLLER
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Brigada Yana Syrovoga Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
							owner = CONTROLLER
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"3-ya Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
							owner = CONTROLLER
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"4-ya Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
							owner = CONTROLLER
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok" }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok" }
				event_target:Politcenter = {
					division_template = {
						name = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"		# Elite
						regiments = {
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
							infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						}
						support = {
							recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
							field_hospital = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						}
						priority = 2
						is_locked = yes
					}
					random_owned_state = {

							division = "name = \"5-ya Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"

				event_target:Politcenter = {

###Переговоры Семёнова, Сибири и Японии##
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.79
	title = rcw_usfev.79.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.79.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_trilateral_agreement
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { NOT = { has_war_with = BKL } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.79.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.80 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.79.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = JAP_no_accept_SIB }
		}
	}
}

#Трёхсторонний договор
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.80
	title = rcw_usfev.80.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.80.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_trilateral_agreement
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = BKL }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.80.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 999
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = JAP_accept_SIB }
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = JAP_accept_SIB }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = BKL modifier = BKL_no_accept_SIB }
		}
		BKL = {
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.47 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.80.b
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = JAP_accept_SIB }
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = JAP_accept_SIB }
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = BKL modifier = BKL_no_accept_SIB }
		}
		BKL = {
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.81 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.80.c
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = JAP_accept_SIB }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = BKL modifier = BKL_accept_SIB }
		JAP = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = JAP_accept_SIB }
		}
		BKL = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = BKL_accept_SIB }
		}
		create_faction = siberian_alliance
		BKL = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.85
	title = rcw_usfev.85.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.85.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_transbaikal_jap_mission
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.85.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		JAP = { BKL = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_integrated_puppet = yes } }
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = 5
			name = JAP_BKL
		}
		USA = {add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = USA_no_accept_JAP }}
		ENG = {add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = ENT_no_accept_JAP }}
		FRA = {add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = ENT_no_accept_JAP }}
			hidden_effect = {

							}
						}

						}
					}
				}
			}
	}

		trigger = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet } }
	}

		text = rcw_usfev.92.desc_1
		trigger = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MON_offer_to_allience } }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_blackhundred
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.92.a
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet } }
			FROM = { ROOT = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_dominion = yes } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarism }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { FROM = { is_in_faction = yes } }
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM is_faction_leader = yes }
						add_to_faction = ROOT
					}
					else = {
						FROM = { create_faction = siberian_axis add_to_faction = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet clr_country_flag = MON_offer_to_allience }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.92.b
		add_political_power = -50
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet clr_country_flag = MON_offer_to_allience }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				FROM = { has_country_flag = MON_offer_to_puppet }
			}
		}
	}

	title = rcw_usfev.99.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.99.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_all_about_gajda
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.99.a
		random_list = {
			95 = {
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.101 hours = 6 }
			}
			5 = {
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.100 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.99.b
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.101 hours = 6 }
			}
			90 = {
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.100 hours = 6 }
			}
		}
	}
}

###Успешный переворот Гайды###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.100
	title = rcw_usfev.100.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.100.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_all_about_gajda
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.100.a
		set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberalism }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.1 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92354 } set_nationality = PRM }
		if = {
		limit = { RSS = { exists = yes } }
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88162 } set_nationality = RSS }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { SIB = { exists = yes } }
					every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88162 } set_nationality = SIB }
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = { BKL = { exists = yes } }
						every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88162 } set_nationality = BKL }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		OVERLORD = { end_puppet = PRM }
		country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.102 days = 5 }
	}
}

###Гайда требуют особых полномочий###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.102
	title = rcw_usfev.102.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.102.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_all_about_gajda
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.102.a
		create_country_leader = { name = "Radola Gaida" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Radola_Gaida_supreme_ruler.dds" expire = "1953.4.15" ideology = national_syndicalism_ideology traits = { } }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = national_syndicalism }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_syndicalism popularity = 0.15 }
		set_party_name = { ideology = national_syndicalism long_name = PRM_national_syndicalism_party_gajda_long name = PRM_national_syndicalism_party_gajda }
		set_cosmetic_tag = PRM_g
	}
		
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.102.b
		add_political_power = -100
		JAP = {country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.103 days = 1 }}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.102.c
		country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.104 hours = 3 }
	}
}

# Звонок за помощью в Токио от Приморья
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.103
	title = rcw_usfev.103.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.103.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_all_about_gajda
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.103.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = PRM modifier = JAP_Radola_diss }
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92354 } set_nationality = CZE }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_array = {
								array = unrecognized_states
								value = FROM.id
							}
						}
						FROM = {
							THIS_country_will_be_recognized_by_PREV = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.103.b
		PRM = {
			create_country_leader = { name = "Radola Gaida" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Radola_Gaida_supreme_ruler.dds" expire = "1953.4.15" ideology = national_syndicalism_ideology traits = { } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = national_syndicalism }
			add_popularity = { ideology = national_syndicalism popularity = 0.15 }
			set_party_name = { ideology = national_syndicalism long_name = PRM_national_syndicalism_party_gajda_long name = PRM_national_syndicalism_party_gajda }
			set_cosmetic_tag = PRM_g
		}
	}
}

# Контрпереворот Калмыкова
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.104
	title = rcw_usfev.104.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.104.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_kalmykov_coup
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.104.a
		add_political_power = 25
		set_politics = { ruling_party = national_syndicalism }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_syndicalism popularity = 0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.2 }
		add_stability = -0.1
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92354 } retire = yes }
		CZE = { set_country_flag = Radola_Gaida_dead }
		RUS = { set_country_flag = Radola_Gaida_dead }
		SOV = { set_country_flag = Radola_Gaida_dead }
		RSS = { set_country_flag = Radola_Gaida_dead }
		SIB = { set_country_flag = Radola_Gaida_dead }
	}
}

# Переворот в Приморье, если там много красных
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.108
	title = rcw_usfev.108.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.108.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_bolsheviks_coup
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.108.a
		PRM = {
			OVERLORD = { end_puppet = PREV }
			leave_faction = yes
			set_politics = { ruling_party = communism }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Pyotr Derber" ruling_only = no } }
				retire_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
			}
			set_country_flag = political_social_liberals_in_socialist_coalition
			clr_country_flag = political_social_liberals_not_in_liberal_coalition
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88161 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88162 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77405 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77400 } set_nationality = REB }
			create_field_marshal = { name = "Alexandr Krasnoshchyokov" id = 88163  portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SOV/Alexandr_Krasnoshchyokov.dds" traits = { thorough_planner } skill = 2 }
			create_corps_commander = { name = "Arkady Krakovetsky" id = 88165  portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/PRM/Arkady_Krakovetsky.dds" traits = {  } skill = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { any_unit_leader = { has_id = 88164 } } }
				create_corps_commander = { name = "Jacob Tryapitsyn" id = 88164  portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/PRM/Jacob_Tryapitsyn.dds" traits = {  } skill = 2 }
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		JAP = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.109 days = 5 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.108.b #Власть берём, но создаём "буфер"
		PRM = {
			OVERLORD = { end_puppet = PREV }
			leave_faction = yes
			set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberalism }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Pyotr Derber" ruling_only = no } }
				retire_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
			}
			set_country_flag = political_social_liberals_in_socialist_coalition
			clr_country_flag = political_social_liberals_not_in_liberal_coalition
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88161 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88162 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77405 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77400 } set_nationality = REB }
			create_field_marshal = { name = "Alexandr Krasnoshchyokov" id = 88163  portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/SOV/Alexandr_Krasnoshchyokov.dds" traits = { thorough_planner } skill = 2 }
			create_corps_commander = { name = "Arkady Krakovetsky" id = 88165  portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/PRM/Arkady_Krakovetsky.dds" traits = {  } skill = 2 }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { any_unit_leader = { has_id = 88164 } } }
				create_corps_commander = { name = "Jacob Tryapitsyn" id = 88164  portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/PRM/Jacob_Tryapitsyn.dds" traits = {  } skill = 2 }
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		JAP = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.109 days = 5 } }
	}
}

###Реакция Японцев на переворот###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.109
	title = rcw_usfev.109.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.109.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_sibir_uprising
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					PRM = { has_government = communism }
					PRM = { has_government = radical_socialism }
				}
			}
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.109.a
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = USA_no_accept_JAP_PRM }
		add_political_power = -100
		PRM = {
			set_party_name = { ideology = despotism long_name = PRM_despotism_JAP_long name = PRM_despotism_JAP }
			create_country_leader = { name = "Ooy Sigmoto" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/JAP/Ooy_Sigmoto.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = despotism_ideology  traits = { warmonger } }
			every_country = {
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88167 } set_nationality = PRM }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88161 } set_nationality = PRM }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77427 } set_nationality = PRM }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77428 } set_nationality = PRM }
			}
		}
		JAP = { PRM = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_integrated_puppet = yes } }
		PRM = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = despotism
			}
		}
		PRM = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = despotism
				ideology = communism
				size = 0.5
				capital = 560
				states = { 560 561 714 657 655 1038 }
				keep_unit_leaders = { 88161 88162 77405 77400 88167 }
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = PRM_JAP
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = PRM
				has_government = communism
			}
			set_stability = 0.9
			set_war_support = 0.8
			PRM = {
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88163 } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88165 } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19190 } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.109.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					PRM = { has_government = communism }
					PRM = { has_government = radical_socialism }
				}
			}
		}
		PRM = {	country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.110 days = 31 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.109.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 999
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				JAP = { NOT = { has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism } }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		RUS = { annex_country = { target = PRM transfer_troops = yes } }
	}
}


###Николаевский инцидент###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.110
	title = rcw_usfev.110.t
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.110.desc

		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed  has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed  has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.110.desc_1
		trigger = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.110.desc_2
		trigger = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rcw_usfev.110.desc_3
		trigger = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_nicolsk
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRM
		PRM = { has_government = communism }
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					set_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { any_unit_leader = { has_id = 19189 } } #Sergey Lazo
					}
				}
				20 = {
					set_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed
				}
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						NOT = { any_unit_leader = { has_id = 19189 } } #Sergey Lazo
					}
				}
				20 = {
					
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.110.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 999
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Jacob Tryapitsyn" } }
			kill_ideology_leader = radical_socialism
		}
		
		if = {
			limit { OR = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19189 } retire = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit { OR = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed } }
			kill_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.110.b
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { any_unit_leader = { has_id = 88164 } } }
				create_corps_commander = { name = "Jacob Tryapitsyn" id = 88164  portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/PRM/Jacob_Tryapitsyn.dds" traits = {  } skill = 2 }
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = radical_socialism
				size = 0.5
				capital = 560
				states = {
					560
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = PRM
					has_government = radical_socialism
				}
				set_stability = 0.9
				set_war_support = 0.8
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88164 } set_nationality = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit { OR = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19189 } retire = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit { OR = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed } }
			kill_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.110.c
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialism popularity = 0.15 }
		add_ideas = PRM_partisan
		
		if = {
			limit { OR = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19189 } retire = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit { OR = { has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed has_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed } }
			kill_ideology_leader = social_liberalism
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_killed
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Krakoveckiy_killed
			clr_country_flag = rcw_usfev_110_Lazo_n_Krakoveckiy_killed
		}
	}
}

###Анархизация советов###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.111
	title = rcw_usfev.111.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.111.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_tryapitsyn
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRM
		NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism }
		OR = {
			radical_socialism > 0.35
			AND = {
				communism > 0.25
				NOT = { has_government = communism }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = PRM_Bolshevistsky_perevorot_fired }
				radical_socialism > 0.15
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				radical_socialism > 0.35
				has_country_flag = PRM_Bolshevistsky_perevorot_fired
				has_government = communism
				NOT = { communism > 0.25 }
			}
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.111.a
		add_stability = 0.1
		set_politics = { ruling_party = radical_socialism }
		remove_ideas = PRM_partisan
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				radical_socialism > 0.35
				has_country_flag = PRM_Bolshevistsky_perevorot_fired
				has_government = communism
				NOT = { communism > 0.25 }
			}
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.111.b
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialism popularity = -0.05 }
		remove_ideas = PRM_partisan
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.111.c

# Правый переворот в Приморье
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.112
	title = rcw_usfev.112.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.112.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRM
		OR = {
			PRM = { has_government = radical_socialism }
			PRM = { has_government = communism }
		}
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 365
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.112.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 999
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { exists = yes } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19190 } set_nationality = RUS }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { SOV = { exists = yes } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19190 } set_nationality = SOV }
		}
		set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism }
		every_country = {
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88163 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88164 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88165 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88167 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92349 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92350 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92350 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88156 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77405 } set_nationality = PRM }
		}
		load_oob = PRM_contra_2.0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.112.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				RUS = { exists = yes }
				SOV = { exists = yes }
			}
		}
		set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism }
		every_country = {
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88163 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88164 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88165 } set_nationality = REB }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88167 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92349 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92350 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92350 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88156 } set_nationality = PRM }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77405 } set_nationality = PRM }
		}
		load_oob = PRM_contra_2.0
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { exists = yes } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19190 } set_nationality = RUS }
			RUS = { change_tag_from = PRM }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { SOV = { exists = yes } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 19190 } set_nationality = SOV }
			SOV = { change_tag_from = PRM }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.112.c
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = fascism
			size = 0.5
			capital = 408
			states = {
				408 714 657 655 1034 1035
			}
			keep_unit_leaders = {
				88163 88164 88165 19190
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = PRM
				has_government = fascism
			}
			set_stability = 0.9
			set_war_support = 0.8
			every_country = {
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88167 } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92349 } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92350 } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 92350 } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88156 } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77405 } set_nationality = PREV.PREV }
			}
			load_oob = PRM_contra_2.0
		}
	}
}

	title = rcw_usfev.113.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.113.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_derber_and_vologodsky
	
	trigger = {
		tag = PRM
		is_subject = no
		SIB = { exists = yes NOT = { has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism } }
		RUS = { has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.113.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 999
		}
		SIB = {
			SIB = { PRM = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_semi_independent = yes } }
			PRM = {
				every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77400 } } set_nationality = SIB }
				#set_politics = {
					#ruling_party = social_liberalism
				#}
			set_popularities = {
						national_syndicalism = 1
						despotism = 10
						fascism = 5
						radical_socialism = 6
						authoritarism = 10
						social_democracy = 10
						social_liberalism = 23
						market_liberalism = 10
						social_conservatism = 15
						communism = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.113.b
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.117
	title = rcw_usfev.117.t
	desc = {
	text = rcw_usfev.117.d_not
	trigger = {NOT = { controls_state = 651} NOT = {controls_state = 653} }
	}
	desc = {
	text = rcw_usfev.117.d_ekat
	trigger = { controls_state = 653 }
	}
	desc = {
	text = rcw_usfev.117.d_ufa
	trigger = { controls_state = 651 }
	}
	desc = {
	text = rcw_usfev.117.d_ufa_ekat
	trigger = { AND = { controls_state = 653 } AND = { controls_state = 651} }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_new_capital
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SIB_right_oficers
				days = 200
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.117.a
		set_capital = 571
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberalism popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = despotism popularity = 0.05 }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = 2
		}
		country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.120 days = 10 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 999
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.119
	title = rcw_usfev.119.t
	desc = { text = rcw_usfev.119.d_adm trigger = {check_variable = { directory_balance > 1 }}}
	desc = { text = rcw_usfev.119.d_kad trigger = {check_variable = { directory_balance < 1 }}}
	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = economy_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = security_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_intel_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = military_minister_trait
			remove_ideas_with_trait = army_chief
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.119.a
		trigger = { check_variable = { directory_balance > 1 } }
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		set_party_name = { ideology = despotism long_name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = social_democracy long_name = RUS_social_democracy_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_democracy_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = social_liberalism long_name = RUS_social_liberalism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_liberalism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = market_liberalism long_name = RUS_market_liberalism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_market_liberalism_kolchak_party }
		add_popularity = { ideology = despotism popularity = 0.15 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberalism popularity = 0.05 }
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88152 } set_nationality = REB }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberalism }
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nekrasov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Nikolay_Nekrasov.dds" expire = "1975.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = { } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = social_democracy elections_allowed = no }
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Chernov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Victor_Chernov_ALT.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_democracy_ideology traits = { } }
			create_country_leader = { name = "Alexandr Clafton" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Alexandr_Clafton.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = { min_2_biased_intellectual liberal_journalist silent_workhorse } }
			create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Pepelyaev" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Victor_Pepelyaev.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = { } }
			create_country_leader = { name = "Vyacheslav Volkov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Vyacheslav_Volkov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { min_1_supreme_ruler staunch_monarchist anti_democrat warmonger } }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 88166 } } set_nationality = REB }
			load_focus_tree = Russia_Russian_state_Kolchak_focus
		}
		set_politics = { ruling_party = despotism elections_allowed = no }
		clear_variable = directory_balance
		remove_ideas = RSS_disjointed_government
		add_ideas = RSS_disjointed_government_after
		add_ideas = {
			Pyotr_Vologodsky_1
			Yuri_Klyuchnikov_2
			Ivan_Mikhailov_3
			Alexander_Gattenberger_4
			Sergey_Starynkevich_5
			Nikolay_Stepanov_6
			Vasily_Markovsky_army_chief
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.119.a
		trigger = {check_variable = { directory_balance < 1 }}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberalism popularity = -0.1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberalism popularity = 0.15 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = despotism popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarism popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberalism }
			retire_country_leader = yes
		}
		set_party_name = { ideology = despotism long_name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_authoritarism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = social_democracy long_name = RUS_social_democracy_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_democracy_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = social_liberalism long_name = RUS_social_liberalism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_liberalism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = market_liberalism long_name = RUS_market_liberalism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_market_liberalism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = social_conservatism long_name = RUS_social_conservatism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_conservatism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarism long_name = RUS_despotism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_despotism_kolchak_party }
		set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = RUS_fascism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_fascism_kolchak_party }

			limit = { OCH = { exists = yes } }

				random_list = {
					40 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.122
					}
					20 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.123
					}

				factor = 999
				FROM = { is_ai = yes }
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}

		name = rcw_usfev.124.b
		add_to_variable = {
			var = directory_balance
			value = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { OCH = { exists = yes } }
			OCH = { country_event = rcw_usfev.128 }
			else = {
				random_list = {
					70 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.126
					}
					30 = {
						country_event = rcw_usfev.125
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
}

	id = rcw_usfev.143

	desc = rcw_usfev.143.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rss_kolchak_finances
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.143.a
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				fall_2_hyper_inflation = yes
			}
			25 = {
				rise_hyper_inflation = yes
			}
			25 = {
				rise_2_hyper_inflation = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.143.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = hyper_inflation_1
			}
			remove_ideas = hyper_inflation_1
			add_timed_idea = { idea = hyper_inflation_1 days = 70 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = hyper_inflation_2
			}
			remove_ideas = hyper_inflation_2
			add_timed_idea = { idea = hyper_inflation_2 days = 140 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = hyper_inflation_3
			}
			remove_ideas = hyper_inflation_3
			add_timed_idea = { idea = hyper_inflation_3 days = 210 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = hyper_inflation_4
			}
			remove_ideas = hyper_inflation_4
			add_timed_idea = { idea = hyper_inflation_4 days = 280 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = hyper_inflation_5
			}
			remove_ideas = hyper_inflation_5
			add_timed_idea = { idea = hyper_inflation_5 days = 350 }
		}
	}

			}

		}

		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #А чоб собсна нет?
		name = rcw_usfev.148.a
		ROOT = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = sazonov_cca_2 }
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.149 }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = unrecognized_states
						value = FROM.id
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					THIS_country_will_be_recognized_by_PREV = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Ну а я не хочу
		name = rcw_usfev.148.b
		ROOT = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = sazonov_cca_3 }
		}
		FROM= { country_event = rcw_usfev.150 }
	}
	
}

	desc = rcw_usfev.156.desc

		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		OR = {
			tag = BKL
			tag = BRY
			tag = SIB
			is_main_former_russian_empire_country = yes
		}
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = BKL_government_of_the_REO
			NOT = { has_focus_tree = Transbaikal_white_cossaks_focus has_focus_tree = Transbaikal_white_cossaks_late_focus }
		}
		MON = { exists = yes has_government = despotism any_neighbor_country = { any_other_country = { has_war_with = PREV has_government = communism } } }
		any_unit_leader = { has_id = 77402 }
		NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Roman Fyodorovich von Ungern-Sternberg" ruling_only = yes } }
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialism
			has_government = communism
			has_government = social_democracy
			has_government = social_liberalism
			surrender_progress > 0.69
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.156.a
		add_war_support = -0.1
		add_manpower = -2000
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 } } set_nationality = REB }
		MON = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.157 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.156.b
