	title = rcw_usfev.159.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.159.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_czechoslovakians
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.159.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		CCA = { add_ideas = SIB_CCA_border }
		SIB = { add_ideas = SIB_CCA_border }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.159.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		if = {
		limit = { tag = CCA }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SIB
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
		limit = { tag = SIB }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = CCA
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
}

###Чехословаки отказываются вести боевые действия между собой###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.160
	title = rcw_usfev.160.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.160.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_czechoslovakians
	
	trigger = {
		OR = { is_former_russian_empire_settled_non_cossack_country = yes former_russian_empire_cossack_country = yes }
		OR = {
			has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
			has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
			has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
		}
		any_other_country = {
			has_war_with = ROOT
			OR = {
				has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
				has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
				has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.160.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
					has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
					has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
				}
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Dal'niy Vostok"
			}
			delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
			}
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 92354 } } set_nationality = CZE }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 88153 } } set_nationality = CZE }
			every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 92355 } } set_nationality = CZE }
		}
	}
}

			set_nationality = JAP

	}

	desc = rcw_usfev.174.desc

			hidden_effect = {

				random_list = {
						30 = {
							country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.175 days = 1 }
						}
						60 = {
							country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.176 days = 1 }
						}
						10 = {
							country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.177 days = 1 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { SIB = { exists = yes } }
				hidden_effect = {
				SIB = {
					random_list = {
							30 = {
								country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.175 days = 1 }
							}
							60 = {
								country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.176 days = 1 }
							}
							10 = {
								country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.177 days = 1 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

###Унгерн возвращается на родину, если война ещё не проиграна###
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.178
	title = rcw_usfev.178.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.178.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_ungern_WAAAR
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = MON
		has_country_leader = { name = "Roman Fyodorovich von Ungern-Sternberg" ruling_only = yes }
		has_war = no
		has_civil_war = no
		any_neighbor_country = {
			exists = yes
			OR = { is_former_russian_empire_settled_non_cossack_country = yes former_russian_empire_cossack_country = yes }
			has_capitulated = no
			is_subject = no
			NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			surrender_progress < 0.4
			NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism }
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.178.a
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = REB }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		add_ideas = limited_monarchy_gov_form
		add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
		remove_ideas = help_from_foreign_interventionists
		delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			division_template = "Cavaleriyskaya brigada"
		}
		every_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				OR = { is_former_russian_empire_settled_non_cossack_country = yes former_russian_empire_cossack_country = yes }
				has_capitulated = no
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				surrender_progress < 0.4
				NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism }
			}
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.179 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.178.b
		trigger = { always = no }
	}

}

	id = rcw_usfev.179

	desc = rcw_usfev.179.desc

		REB = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { OR = { has_id = 77402 has_id = 77447 has_id = 77448 has_id = 77449 } } set_nationality = ROOT } }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarism popularity = 0.02 }
		add_manpower = 2000
		ROOT = { MON = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_colony = yes } }
		division_template = {
			name = "Kavaleriyskaya Diviziya"	# Cavalry

				cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				cavalry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			}
			support = {
				recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
				engineer = { x = 0 y = 1 }
			}
		}
		capital_scope = {
			create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Otryad Ungerna\" division_template = \"Kavaleriyskaya Diviziya\" start_experience_factor = 1 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
					owner = ROOT
				}
		}
	}

# Союз с генералами у КОМУЧа
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.191
	title = rcw_usfev.191.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.191.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.191.a
		FROM = {
			create_faction = CCA_VSUR_alt
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				leave_faction = yes
				FROM = { add_to_faction = PREV }
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
			else = {
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		FROM = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.191.b
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

# Переговоры об объединении
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.192
	title = rcw_usfev.192.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.192.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Они должны подчиниться
		trigger = {
			strength_ratio = {
				tag = RVA
				ratio > 1
			}
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.192.a
		add_political_power = -50
		set_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_supp
		RVA = { country_event = rcw_usfev.193 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			RSS = { exists = no }

		}

		}
		name = rcw_usfev.192.c

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.193
	title = rcw_usfev.193.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.193.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_prm_diterikhs_coup
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_supp } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcw_usfev_193_desc_1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_unite } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcw_usfev_193_desc_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_surr } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcw_usfev_193_desc_3
		}
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.193.a
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_supp } }
			FROM = { clr_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_supp }
			every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = FROM }
			FROM = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = despotism
					popularity = 0.04
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarism
					popularity = 0.04
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = ROOT
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_unite } }
			FROM = { clr_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_unite }
			hidden_effect = {
				RSS = {
					set_party_name = { ideology = radical_socialism long_name = CCA_radical_socialism_party_long name = CCA_radical_socialism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = social_democracy long_name = CCA_social_democracy_party_long name = CCA_social_democracy_party }

					set_party_name = { ideology = social_conservatism long_name = RVA_social_conservatism_party_long name = RVA_social_conservatism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarism long_name = RVA_authoritarism_party_long name = RVA_authoritarism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = despotism long_name = RVA_despotism_party_long name = RVA_despotism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = RVA_fascism_party_long name = RVA_fascism_party }
					set_party_name = { ideology = national_syndicalism long_name = RVA_national_syndicalism_party_long name = RVA_national_syndicalism_party }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Mark Natanson" desc = RUS_Mark_Andreevich_Natanson_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Mark_Natanson.dds" expire = "1923.7.29" ideology = narodnichestvo  traits = { min_1_old_guy min_1_naive_optimist isolationist_revolutionary } }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Valerian Kuibyshev" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SOV/Valerian_Kuibyshev.dds" expire = "1935.1.25" ideology = marxism traits = { min_1_totalist_chairman veteran_communist } }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Ivan Mayskiy" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Ivan_Maisky.dds" expire = "1975.1.1" ideology = social_democracy_ideology  traits = { min_2_great_compromiser  } }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Vladimir Volskiy" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Vladimir_Volsky.dds" expire = "1937.10.4" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = { min_1_happy_amateur figurehead_president silent_workhorse } }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Pavel Milyukov" desc = RUS_Pavel_Milyukov_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Pavel_Milyukov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = market_liberalism_ideology traits = { historian political_dancer liberal_journalist min_1_popular_figurehead the_gentleman_president } }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail Rodzyanko" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Mikhail_Rodzyanko.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = { political_dancer min_1_power_hungry_demagogue figurehead_president min_1_popular_figurehead conservative_nationalist } }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Vladimir Purishkevich" desc = RUS_Vladimir_Pushkevich_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Vladimir_Pushkevich.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = fascism_ideology  traits = { staunch_monarchist dislike_jew fascist_militia_leader political_dancer min_1_power_hungry_demagogue min_1_popular_figurehead anti_democrat } }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Boris Savinkov" desc = RUS_Boris_Savinkov_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Boris_Savinkov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = national_syndicalism_ideology  traits = { dictator ideological_crusader adventurous_daredevil political_dancer min_1_popular_figurehead min_4_prince_of_terror } }
					create_country_leader = { name = "Anton Denikin" desc = RUS_Anton_Denikin_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Anton_Denikin.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = despotism_ideology traits = { warmonger great_war_hero min_1_old_general silent_workhorse dislikes_germany } }
					if = {
						limit = { CCA = { has_country_leader = { name = "Victor Chernov" ruling_only = no } } }
						create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Chernov" desc = RUS_Victor_Chernov_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Victor_Chernov_ALT.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology  traits = {  } }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { RVA = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexeev_dead } } }
						create_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail Alexeev" desc = RUS_Mikhail_Alexeev_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Mikhail_Alexeev.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = despotism_ideology traits = { warmonger } }
					}
				}
				ROOT = { save_global_event_target_as = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MAJOR initiate_verification_of_the_popularity_of_coalitions = yes capital_scope = { set_state_flag = new_capital } }
				FROM = { save_global_event_target_as = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MINOR initiate_verification_of_the_popularity_of_coalitions = yes }
				RSS = { save_global_event_target_as = UNITED_COUNTRY random_state = { limit = { OR = { is_owned_by = ROOT is_owned_by = FROM } } PREV = { set_state_owner = PREV } } set_cosmetic_tag = RSS_VLG_DON } #load_focus_tree = Russia_Russian_state_directory_focus
				RSS = { inherit_technology = ROOT }
				RSS = { inherit_technology = FROM }
				party_populatiry_addition_script_1 = yes
				set_ruling_party_for_uniting_country_script = yes
				country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1918 hours = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_surr } }
			FROM = { clr_country_flag = CCA_RVA_unite_surr }
			FROM = { every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = FROM
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = FROM
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = FROM }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = RSS_VLG_DON
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.193.b

		FROM = { country_event = rcw_usfev.194 }

		tag = RUS

		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired

		has_country_flag =  Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_Ekat
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead
			OR = {
				has_full_control_of_state = 653
				has_full_control_of_state = 573
				has_full_control_of_state = 572
			}
			CCA = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue }
			SIB = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue }
			RVA = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue }
			MCW = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 20
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.200.a
		#news_event

			factor = 1
		}

		set_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead
		set_country_flag = Alexandra_Fyodorovna_Romanova_dead

			factor = 0
		}

	}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.204
	title = rcw_usfev.204.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.204.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_comre_reorgonize_of_headquarters
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		every_country = {
			clr_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue
			clr_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here
		}
		set_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue
		set_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here
	}
	
	option = { #Николай, Николай, Коооляяяя.....
		name = rcw_usfev.204.a
		hidden_effect = { remove_authoritarism_leader = yes }
		create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" desc = RUS_Nikolay_II_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Nikolay_II_Romanov_military.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { inexperienced_imperialist } }
		create_field_marshal = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" id = 77401 portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Nikolay_II_Romanov_military.dds" traits = { old_guard } skill = 1 attack_skill = 2 defense_skill = 2 planning_skill = 2 logistics_skill = 2 }
		remove_ideas = RUS_Nikolay_II_idea
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_ideas = absolute_monarchy_gov_form
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.204.b
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Vladimir Cappel" ruling_only = yes } } }

		add_ideas = RUS_Nikolay_II_idea
	}

	option = { #А чоб собсна нет?
		name = rcw_usfev.206.a
		ROOT = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CCA modifier = sazonov_cca_2 }
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		CCA = {country_event = rcw_usfev.207}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = unrecognized_states
						value = FROM.id
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					THIS_country_will_be_recognized_by_PREV = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Ну а я не хочу
		name = rcw_usfev.206.b
		ROOT = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = CCA modifier = sazonov_cca_3 }
		}
		CCA = { country_event = rcw_usfev.208 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.214
	title = rcw_usfev.214.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.214.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_Nikolai2_CCA_devil_return
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = right_monarcical_reaction_right_side }
		name = rcw_usfev.214.a
		hidden_effect = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = despotism
				states = { 573 }
				size = 1
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
			}
			ROOT = { transfer_state = 573 }
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = news_n.31 hours = 48 } }
		every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 88150 } promote_leader = yes }
		set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarism }
		ROOT = { save_global_event_target_as = CCA_CW_right }
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = { name = "Vladimir Cappel" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Vladimir_Cappel.dds" expire = "1953.07.22" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { min_1_old_general staunch_monarchist min_2_ideological_crusader anti_democrat } }
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = social_liberalism
				size = 0.3
				keep_unit_leaders = { 88150 }
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ROOT
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = CCA_CW_eser
			}
			event_target:CCA_CW_eser = {
				load_focus_tree = Committee_of_Members_of_the_Constituent_Assembly_focus
				if = {
					limit = { RUS = { exists = yes OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } } }
					declare_war_on = {
						target = RUS
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:CCA_CW_right = {
				add_ideas = military_dictatorship_gov_form
				load_focus_tree = His_Imperial_Majesty_Military_Committee_focus
			}
		}

				name = "Monarhicheskaya Brigada"
				regiments = {
					militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { CCA_CW_right_forces_temp = ROOT.CCA_CW_right_forces }
			spawn_right_units_in_CCA_CW_cycle = yes
		}
		event_target:CCA_CW_eser = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Narodnoarmeyskaya Brigada"
				regiments = {
					militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
				is_locked = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { CCA_CW_eser_forces_temp = ROOT.CCA_CW_eser_forces }
			spawn_eser_units_in_CCA_CW_cycle = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { event_target:CCA_CW_eser = { has_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e" } check_variable = { CCA_CZE_support > 2 } }
			event_target:CCA_CW_eser = {
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit= {
						division = "name = \"1-ya Brigada Stanislava Checheka Chekhoslovatskogo legiona\" division_template = \"Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 1 start_manpower_factor = 1"
						owner = event_target:CCA_CW_eser_forces
					}
					create_unit= {

						owner = event_target:CCA_CW_eser_forces
					}
					create_unit= {

						owner = event_target:CCA_CW_eser_forces
					}

					division_template = "Brigada Chekhoslovatskogo legiona Povolzh'e"
				}
			}
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = right_monarcical_reaction_right_side
		clr_country_flag = right_monarcical_reaction_eser_side
		clear_variable = CCA_CZE_support
		clear_variable = CCA_CW_right_forces
		clear_variable = CCA_CW_eser_forces
	}
}

# Захват Николая II Сибирью
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.251
	title = rcw_usfev.251.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.251.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_rcw_Nikolai2_CCA
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SIB
			tag = RSS
			tag = RVA
		}
		controls_state = 653
		RUS = { has_country_flag =  Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_Ekat NOT = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead } }
		NOT = { CCA = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue } }
		NOT = { SIB = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue } }
		NOT = { RVA = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.251.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { tag = SIB } }
			create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" desc = RUS_Nikolay_II_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Nikolay_II_ALT2.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { inexperienced_imperialist weak_character} }
		}
		RUS = { clr_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_Ekat }
		set_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue
		set_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarism popularity = 0.10 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservatism popularity = 0.10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.251.b
		trigger = { has_government = social_liberalism }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		RUS = { clr_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_Ekat }
		country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.202 days = 1 }
	}
}

# Русская Вандея
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.252
	title = rcw_usfev.252.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.252.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_long_live_the_dmitry
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_is_here }
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_is_here }
			NOT = { RUS = { has_country_flag = Dmitriy_Pavlovich_Romanov_dead } has_country_flag = Dmitriy_Pavlovich_Romanov_is_here }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.252.a #Дело Романовых продолжается
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead } } NOT = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.254 days = 1 } }
					30 = { }
				}
				else = {
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { OR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here any_unit_leader = { has_id = 77401 } } }
						country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.253 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_dead } } NOT = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_is_here } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay III Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nikolaevich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.255 days = 1 } }
					30 = { }
				}
				else = {
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { OR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay III Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nikolaevich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_flag = Nikolay_Nikolayevich_Romanov_is_here any_unit_leader = { has_id = 76836 } } }
						country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.253 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_dead } } NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
					NOT = { any_country = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } } }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.256 days = 1 } }
					30 = { }
				}
				else = {
					random_other_country = {
						limit = { OR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail II Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes } has_country_flag = Mikhail_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here any_unit_leader = { has_id = 77410 } } }
						country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.253 days = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_dead } } NOT = { has_country_flag = Kirill_Vladimirovich_Romanov_is_here } }
			if = {

				}

					30 = { }

				else = {

						country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.253 days = 1 }

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.253
	title = rcw_usfev.253.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.253.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_long_live_the_dmitry
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.253.a #Час пробил!
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
				}
			}
			FROM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.254 days = 2 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay III Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nikolaevich Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
				}
			}
			FROM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.255 days = 2 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail II Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Mikhail Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
				}
			}
			FROM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.256 days = 2 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Kirill I Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Kirill Vladimirovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
				}
			}
			FROM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.257 days = 2 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Dmitriy II Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
					has_country_leader = { name = "Dmitriy Pavlovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
				}
			}
			FROM = { country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.258 days = 2 } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 4
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				original_tag = CCA
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.252.b #У каждого свой участок борьбы
		add_political_power = -50
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}
# Ники 2
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.254
	title = rcw_usfev.254.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.254.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sib_long_live_the_dmitry
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.254.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarism popularity = 0.03 }
		FROM = { clr_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here }
		set_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_is_here
		FROM = { remove_ideas = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_army_chief }
		FROM = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77401 } set_nationality = ROOT } }
		REB = { every_unit_leader = { limit = { has_id = 77401 } set_nationality = ROOT } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
						has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { original_tag = CCA } }
				FROM = {
					transfer_units_fraction= {
						target = ROOT
						size = 1
						stockpile_ratio = 1
						army_ratio = 1
						navy_ratio = 1
						air_ratio = 1
					}
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = FROM
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				else = { FROM = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_puppet = yes retire_country_leader = yes } }
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = { OR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" ruling_only = no } has_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Alexandrovich Romanov" ruling_only = no } } }
						retire_ideology_leader = authoritarism
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				else = { FROM = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_puppet = yes retire_country_leader = yes } }
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					every_country = {
						limit = { OR = { has_country_leader = { name = "Dmitriy II Romanov" ruling_only = no } has_country_leader = { name = "Dmitriy Pavlovich Romanov" ruling_only = no } } }
						retire_ideology_leader = authoritarism
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_bkl_balagats
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BKL_Burnatcom_was_disbanded }
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcw_usfev_331_desc_tt
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.331.a
		remove_ideas = BKL_balagat_movement
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = BKL_balagat_movement_1 }
		country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.332 days = 60 }
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.331.b
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = BKL_balagat_movement }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = BKL_balagat_movement
				add_idea = BKL_balagat_movement_1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.331.c
		remove_ideas = BKL_balagat_movement
		add_timed_idea = { idea = BKL_balagat_movement days = 180 }
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { has_country_flag = BKL_Burnatcom_was_disbanded }
		name = rcw_usfev.331.d
		BRY = {
			transfer_state = 564
		}
		puppet = BRY
		BRY = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarism
			}
			set_popularities = {
				authoritarism = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

# Восстание Толстихина
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.342
	title = rcw_usfev.342.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.342.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_bkl_tolstikhin_revolt
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = BKL
		is_subject = no
		has_completed_focus = BKL_provisional_regional_government
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = BKL_confrontation_to_the_siberian_government
			has_idea = BKL_confiscation_idea
		}
		has_civil_war = no
		has_war = yes
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			has_idea = BKL_confiscation_idea
			has_completed_focus = BKL_cargo_requisition
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_war_with = SIB
				has_war_with = RSS
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.342.a
		create_country_leader = { name = "Ivan Tolstikhin" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/BKL/Ivan_Tolstikhin.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = { } }
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = social_liberalism
			size = 0.2
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger  = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { NOT = { original_tag = BKL  tag = SIB tag = RSS} has_war_with = BKL }
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { tag = BKL has_government = social_liberalism }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_other_country = { OR = { tag = RSS tag = SIB } has_war_with = RUS NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } } }
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = RSS tag = SIB } has_war_with = RUS NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
				random_other_country = {
					limit = { tag = BKL has_government = social_liberalism }
					subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_semi_independent = yes
				}
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = { tag = BKL has_government = social_liberalism }
			load_focus_tree = Transbaikal_Chita_eser_focus
			set_country_flag = BKL_not_white_cossaks_focus
			save_global_event_target_as = BKL_CW
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { OR = { has_id = 77404 has_id = 77405 has_id = 77406 } }
			set_nationality = event_target:BKL_CW
		}
		event_target:BKL_CW = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_id = 77404 has_id = 77405 has_id = 77406 } }
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = BKL_CW
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.342.b
		create_country_leader = { name = "Ivan Tolstikhin" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/BKL/Ivan_Tolstikhin.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = { } }
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = social_liberalism
			size = 0.2
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger  = {
				always = yes
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { NOT = { original_tag = BKL  tag = SIB tag = RSS } has_war_with = BKL }
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { tag = BKL has_government = social_liberalism }
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { any_other_country = { OR = { tag = RSS tag = SIB } has_war_with = RUS NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } } }
			random_other_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = RSS tag = SIB } has_war_with = RUS NOT = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
				random_other_country = {
					limit = { tag = BKL has_government = social_liberalism }
					subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_semi_independent = yes
				}
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = { tag = BKL has_government = social_liberalism }
			load_focus_tree = Transbaikal_Chita_eser_focus
			set_country_flag = BKL_not_white_cossaks_focus
			save_global_event_target_as = BKL_CW
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { OR = { has_id = 77404 has_id = 77405 has_id = 77406 } }
			set_nationality = event_target:BKL_CW
		}
		event_target:BKL_CW = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_id = 77404 has_id = 77405 has_id = 77406 } }
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = BKL_CW
		random_other_country = {
			limit = { tag = BKL has_government = social_liberalism }
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# Государство Бурят-Монголия
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.349
	title = rcw_usfev.349.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.349.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_bkl_hambo-lama
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Grigory Semyonov" ruling_only = yes } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = rcw_usfev_349_tt
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.349.a
		BRY = {
			transfer_state = 564
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_liberalism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberalism
				popularity = 0.3
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_offensive_war_with = ROOT
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = BRY
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_defensive_war_with = ROOT
					NOT = { has_war_with = BRY }
				}
				BRY = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
		transfer_units_fraction= {
			target = BRY
			size = 1
			stockpile_ratio = 1
			army_ratio = 1
			navy_ratio = 1
			air_ratio = 1
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		BRY = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Grigory Semyonov" ruling_only = yes }
		}
		name = rcw_usfev.349.b
		BRY = {
			transfer_state = 564
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = despotism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = despotism
				popularity = 0.3
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_offensive_war_with = ROOT
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = BRY
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_defensive_war_with = ROOT
					NOT = { has_war_with = BRY }
				}
				BRY = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = PREV
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = { name = "Grigory Semyonov" desc = RUS_Grigory_Semenov_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/BKL/Grigory_Semyonov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = despotism_ideology traits = { inexperienced_imperialist spirit_of_genghis } }
		}
		transfer_units_fraction= {
			target = BRY
			size = 1
			stockpile_ratio = 1
			army_ratio = 1
			navy_ratio = 1
			air_ratio = 1
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		BRY = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 999
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.350

	hidden = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		tag = BKL
		NOT = { has_completed_focus = BKL_chita_military_school }
		OR = {
			has_focus_tree = Transbaikal_white_cossaks_focus
			has_focus_tree = Transbaikal_white_cossaks_late_focus
		}
		NOT = {
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_10
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_9
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_8
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_7
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_6
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_5
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_4
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_3
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_2
			has_idea = lack_of_officers_1
		}
		has_army_manpower = {
			size > 12000
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		add_ideas = lack_of_officers_8
	}
}

# Военный переворот в Приморье
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.352
	title = rcw_usfev.352.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.352.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_bkl_hambo-lama
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.352.a
		OVERLORD = { end_puppet = ROOT }
		FROM = { puppet = ROOT }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.352.b
		
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		add_manpower = -500
		add_stability = -0.1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# Читинский эндшпиль
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.353
	title = rcw_usfev.353.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.353.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sov_redarm
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.353.a
		FROM = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = FROM }
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes FROM = { is_ai = no } }
			change_tag_from = FROM
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = FROM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
	}
}

# Отмена японских кредитов

		tag = BKL

		days = 1
	}

		add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = -1 }
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -1 }
	}
}

# Российская Республика для КОМУЧа
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1915
	title = rcw_usfev.1915.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1915.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sov_redarm
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1915.a
		hidden_effect = {
			CCA = { save_global_event_target_as = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MAJOR save_global_event_target_as = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MINOR capital_scope = { set_state_flag = new_capital } }
			RSS = { save_global_event_target_as = UNITED_COUNTRY transfer_state = 581 set_cosmetic_tag = RSS_All_russian_provisional_government }
			RSS = { inherit_technology = CCA }
			RSS = { inherit_technology = SIB }
			party_populatiry_addition_script_1 = yes
			set_ruling_party_for_uniting_country_script = yes
			country_event = { id = rcw_usfev.1919 hours = 1 }
			
			CCA = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = CCA_replace_soviets_on_zemstvos_idea }
					#####RSS = { add_ideas = CCA_replace_soviets_on_zemstvos_idea }
					RSS = { add_timed_idea = { idea = CCA_replace_soviets_on_zemstvos_idea days = 365 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = CCA_workers_questions_idea }
					#####RSS = { add_ideas = CCA_workers_questions_idea }
					RSS = { add_timed_idea = { idea = CCA_workers_questions_idea days = 365 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = CCA_mobilization_idea }
					#####RSS = { add_ideas = CCA_mobilization_idea }
					RSS = { add_timed_idea = { idea = CCA_mobilization_idea days = 365 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = CCA_consular_citizen_idea }
					#####RSS = { add_ideas = CCA_consular_citizen_idea }
					RSS = { add_timed_idea = { idea = CCA_consular_citizen_idea days = 365 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = CCA_hunta_idea }
					#####RSS = { add_ideas = CCA_hunta_idea }
					RSS = { add_timed_idea = { idea = CCA_hunta_idea days = 365 } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = Entente_credit_for_Russia }
					RSS = { add_ideas = Entente_credit_for_Russia }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = help_from_foreign_interventionists }
					RSS = { add_ideas = help_from_foreign_interventionists }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { URL = { is_subject_of = CCA } }
				RSS = {
					annex_country = { 
						target = URL
						transfer_troops = no 
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { URL = { is_subject_of = SIB } }
				RSS = {
					annex_country = { 
						target = URL
						transfer_troops = no 
					}
				}
			}
			
			create_country_leader = { name = "Vyacheslav Volkov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Vyacheslav_Volkov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { min_1_supreme_ruler staunch_monarchist anti_democrat warmonger } }
			
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue }
				RSS = {
					create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" desc = RUS_Nikolay_II_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Nikolay_II_ALT2.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { inexperienced_imperialist weak_character } }
				}
			}
			
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = RUS NOT = { is_on_continent = europe is_on_continent = middle_east } }
				add_core_of = RSS
			}
		}
	}
}

							set_party_name = { ideology = social_conservatism long_name = RUS_social_conservatism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_social_conservatism_kolchak_party }
							set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarism long_name = RUS_despotism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_despotism_kolchak_party }
							set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = RUS_fascism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_fascism_kolchak_party }
							set_party_name = { ideology = national_syndicalism long_name = RUS_national_syndicalism_kolchak_party_long name = RUS_national_syndicalism_kolchak_party }
							set_politics = { ruling_party = social_liberalism elections_allowed = no }
							retire_country_leader = yes
							retire_country_leader = yes
							create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay Nekrasov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Nikolay_Nekrasov.dds" expire = "1975.1.1" ideology = social_liberalism_ideology traits = { } }
							set_politics = { ruling_party = social_democracy elections_allowed = no }
							retire_country_leader = yes
							create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Chernov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Victor_Chernov_ALT.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_democracy_ideology traits = { } }
							create_country_leader = { name = "Alexandr Clafton" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Alexandr_Clafton.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = { min_2_biased_intellectual liberal_journalist silent_workhorse } }
							create_country_leader = { name = "Victor Pepelyaev" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Victor_Pepelyaev.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = social_conservatism_ideology traits = { } }
							create_country_leader = { name = "Vyacheslav Volkov" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SIB/Vyacheslav_Volkov.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { min_1_supreme_ruler staunch_monarchist anti_democrat warmonger } }
							set_politics = {ruling_party = social_conservatism elections_allowed = no}
							load_focus_tree = Russia_Russian_state_Kolchak_focus
							set_country_flag = RSS_Kolchak_from_SIB
							add_ideas = {
								presidential_republic_gov_form
								emergency_laws_b_law
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = Nikolay_Alexandrovich_Romanov_rescue }
					RSS = {
						create_country_leader = { name = "Nikolay II Romanov" desc = RUS_Nikolay_II_DESC picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Nikolay_II_ALT2.dds" expire = "1935.1.1" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = { inexperienced_imperialist weak_character } }
					}
				}
			}
			
			every_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = RUS NOT = { is_on_continent = europe is_on_continent = middle_east } }
				add_core_of = RSS
			}
		}
	}
}

# Объединение двух стран
country_event = {
	id = rcw_usfev.1918
	title = rcw_usfev.1918.t
	desc = rcw_usfev.1918.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_sov_redarm
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	hidden = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rcw_usfev.1918.a
		event_target:UNITED_COUNTRY = {
			set_popularities = {
					radical_socialism = var:radical_socialism_party
					communism = var:communism_party
					social_democracy = var:social_democracy_party
					social_liberalism = var:social_liberalism_party
					market_liberalism = var:market_liberalism_party
					social_conservatism = var:social_conservatism_party
					authoritarism = var:authoritarism_party
					despotism = var:despotism_party
					fascism = var:fascism_party
					national_syndicalism = var:national_syndicalism_party
			}
		}
		THE_GREAT_TWO_COUNTRIES_INTERGRATION_SCRIPT = yes
		random_state = {
			limit = { has_state_flag = new_capital }
			event_target:UNITED_COUNTRY = { set_capital = PREV }
			clr_state_flag = new_capital
		}
		clear_global_event_target = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MAJOR
		clear_global_event_target = INTEGRATING_COUNTRY_MINOR
		clear_global_event_target = UNITED_COUNTRY
	}
}
